lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日出生，汉族，中学学历，籍贯为广东省中山市沙溪镇汇源社区居委会第<span lang="EN-US">40</span>组；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市生命树文化传播有限公司是一家成立于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月的合法企业。因销售圣经播放器，竟然导致傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒被逮捕。中共当局于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，以所谓非法经营罪将他们抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位基督徒都被关押在深圳九围看守所。其家人和律师都被威胁，不得透露案情。后获悉，</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓天永</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被法院判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">邓玉林：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省本溪市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，邓玉林、张莉敏、张鹏柱、胡林、杨丽威五位法轮功学员，向当地民众讲清法轮功被迫害真相，去桓仁县散发法轮功资料，被本溪市国保支队、桓仁县国保大队和普乐堡派出所共计抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，<a name="_Hlk52323402">邓玉林</a>、胡林被关押在桓仁县看守所，张鹏柱被关押于桓仁县拘留所，杨丽威、张莉敏被关押在本溪市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，胡林被转往沈阳法库县看守所关押。胡林最终被判刑两年。从被抓捕开始，胡林一直在绝食抵制迫害，在被迫害的生命垂危的情况下，被法库县看守所走后门强行送往沈阳康家山监狱，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被沈阳康家山监狱迫害致死。本案<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日宣判：邓玉林和杨丽威<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，各罚金二万元，张莉敏<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金一万五千元，张鹏柱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，勒索罚金一万元。邓玉林刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">迪克坦开（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，甘肃省甘南州夏河县拉卜楞寺僧人。藏族人权捍卫者，在押中国良心犯。次成加措、迪克坦开两位拉卜楞寺僧人因与<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日在夏河县发生的大规模僧俗民众的抗议游行，随后被抓捕。次成加措被认为是带头抗议者，在当局对抗议藏人展开大逮捕后出逃，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日于舟曲县遭捕。迪克坦开也于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，被甘南州中级法院一审以“分裂国家罪”秘密判处<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2034</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">迪娜<span lang="EN-US">.</span>依根别尔德：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁市人，伊犁市塔城地区鹤峰县居民，哈萨克族，新疆艺术学院学生，民间知名画家，中国在押政治犯（<span lang="EN-US">CPPC</span>编号：<span lang="EN-US">00704</span>）。曾因两次造访哈萨克国，并其绘画内容主要涉猎浓郁民族特色（即纪念、弘扬哈萨克游牧民族出现过的英雄们，以及具有民族风情的哈萨克毡房和哈萨克草原等），遂于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月被新疆伊犁市当局抓走，送当地某再教育营（又称集中营）接受政治学习教育；后被当地警方以不具名罪由转正式逮捕，并被新疆伊犁市法院秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，罪名不清；据悉，其在集中营学习期间已患严重疾病，后在关押密审期间精神失常；其父多次欲探望女儿，均遭到当局拒绝，且无法获悉其实际所患疾病名称及具体所在监狱地址。目前服刑监狱不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">迪力夏提·吾力拜依：<span lang="EN-US">1</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">962</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市人，哈萨克族名<span lang="EN-US"> Dilshat Oralbai</span>，穆斯林，曾先后任新疆伊犁日报社、伊犁州政治协会、奎屯日报社记者、作家、翻译员、文学总编辑等，哈萨克斯坦国创办企业总负责人，著名新疆媒体人，中国在押良心犯。 自<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年大学毕业起至<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年，曾先后在伊犁日报社、伊犁州政治协会、奎屯日报社工作，担任记者、作家、翻译员、文学总编辑等职务；曾翻译出版、发行<span lang="EN-US">15</span>部文学书籍（含儒勒·凡尔纳的《格兰特船长的儿女》等）、<span lang="EN-US">30</span>余本短篇小说（如《自由》等）及<span lang="EN-US">3</span>部电视剧等，并有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多篇文章在新疆地区多次获奖；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，曾到国外创业，并在哈萨克斯坦国开办企业，自认企业负责人，创办生产塑料窗框和房门的工厂；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年，因听从中共新疆政府要求在外哈萨克族人必须回国，遂与两个妹妹纷纷返回国内；起初两年生活安然如常，<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，迪力夏提·吾力拜依与两个妹妹突然被伊犁州奎屯市警方以不知名罪由抓捕，并送某政治再教育转化营关押，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，其家属接到警方口头通知，知其被伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市法院以不确罪名判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年，其两个妹妹亦遭同等命运，大妹被判<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，小妹被判<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年； 据悉，其因曾做过<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次手术，身体极度虚弱需要及时服药，但在狱中却遭虐待，狱方不仅让其从早到晚不停工作，且拒绝对其进行应有的基本治疗；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2043</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。 目前在新疆生产建设兵团农七师奎屯监狱（新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州奎屯市，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">833200</span>）服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丁国柱：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁抚顺市清原县五名法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日下午，清原县南口前镇法轮功学员丁国柱、徐俊英、张传文及红透山矿的杨秀芳，在清原县敖家堡乡于家堡村给村民们讲法轮功时，被告发到敖家堡乡派出所。后，被清原县国保抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，辽宁抚顺市清原县法院判处丁国柱<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，丁国柱的妻子王海超<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，张传文<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，徐俊英<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半，杨秀芳<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。丁国柱刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">丁汉忠</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，山东省潍坊市昌乐县乔官镇丁家山村村民，退伍军人，抗暴维权者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年因其住宅遭强拆而引发房屋权属争议，双方未达成拆迁安置补偿协议，后其房屋虽被当局非法偷拆和强拆过两次，但因其誓死捍卫，屡次报警，并到镇县政府多次反映逼拆问题而终使家园得以保全，遂引起当地官员的极端仇视。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日其房屋被进行第三次强拆，因来势凶猛，言行蛮横恶劣，差点使其和家人被砸在屋内，随引起冲突，其全家遭暴打群殴，其头颅前部被拆迁方严重铲伤，当即血流如注，头昏眼花。其曾先后<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次报警，但警方却迟迟未到，情急之下其被迫自卫，致使<span lang="EN-US">2</span>名暴力拆迁者受伤，后经抢救无效死亡。其亦因头部伤势过重被送进医院抢救，但很快被赶来的昌乐县警方逮捕。审讯期间，惨遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日其被山东潍坊中级法院以“故意杀人罪”判处死刑，剥权终身。其不服上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日经山东省高院二审，要求撤销一审判决，发回重审。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日再审，最终被以“故意杀人罪”改判为死缓。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，二审维持原判。目前被羁押在潍坊市昌乐县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丁家喜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">北京航空航天大学获得工学学士和工学硕士（飞机制造专业）。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>至<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年在沈阳航空工业总公司、北京航空工业总公司任工程师。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年起转为专职律师，任职于北京市多家律师事务所。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年参与设立北京市德鸿律师事务所任高级合伙人。自<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年起积极参与推动“随迁子女就地高考”教育平权活动。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日与许志永等人发表致习近平等中共高层领导人公开信，要求包括习近平在内的<span lang="EN-US">205</span>名中国部级以上官员率先财产公示。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日丁家喜被当局以“非法集会”罪名刑事拘留，关押在北京市第三看守所。同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，公安机关将丁家喜罪名更换为“寻衅滋事”提交检察院。同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日北京市检察院一分院将案件退回公安局补充侦查，控罪更换为“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，北京市海淀区法院判处丁家喜有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日丁家喜刑满出狱。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点左右，北京人权律师丁家喜在朋友家中被山东国保警察带走，手机等物品被查抄。所涉理由不明。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日遭正式逮捕。至今其代理律师无法会见。丁家喜现关押在山东省临沭县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丁菊英：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1948</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，上海市浦东新区人，原浦东新区唐镇大丰村倪家宅<span lang="EN-US">44</span>号村民，现浦东新区川沙镇华夏东路<span lang="EN-US">2110</span>弄<span lang="EN-US">37</span>号<span lang="EN-US">101</span>室居民，维权反腐公民，人权捍卫者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年，曾因其全家在村中住房遭当局强拆，宅基地（面积<span lang="EN-US">1278</span>平方米）及<span lang="EN-US">4</span>亩承包地亦被政府以“征地”为名掠夺，而过低的拆迁补偿金使其根本买不起高价安置房，随被迫到北京申诉，故而屡遭地方当局无情打压；曾被上海市警方<span lang="EN-US">24</span>次送进看守所和拘留所，被关黑监狱<span lang="EN-US">400</span>多次；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，曾因进京投诉而被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“扰乱社会秩序”罪由刑拘，期满后又被转关押黑监狱数日；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，曾因到浦东新区塘镇信访办协商解决征地拆迁问题，而被当地警方从川沙镇华夏东路的住地以不知名罪由带走，处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，曾因与其他维权人士共同呼吁当局释放所有在押政治犯，及为争取中国民主自由发声呼吁，而被浦东新区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，中共两会召开前期，因被当局视为维稳对象及“不安定分子”，随再次被上海市浦东新区警方以不知名罪由刑事拘留；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被浦东新区张江地区检察院以涉嫌“扰乱国家机关工作秩序罪”转正式批捕，至今未予释放。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日传来了新的消息，为丁菊英作辩护的律师告知丁家属，丁菊英（<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>）沪<span lang="EN-US">0115</span>刑初<span lang="EN-US">746</span>号案，涉嫌“扰乱国家机关工作秩序罪”已被上海市浦东新区法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，没有公开开庭审理。据了解，丁菊英准备依法上诉。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。目前被羁押于浦东新区看守所（上海市浦东新区华益路<span lang="EN-US">351</span>号，邮政编码<span lang="EN-US">: 201210</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丁雪梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南省信阳市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，河南省信阳市法轮功学员陶玉华、杨成云、丁雪梅、白国显、李俊华、杨山萍六人被确山县警察非捕，同时被抢走多部电脑、打印机、真相资料、耗材等物品。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，驻马店驿城区法院宣判。丁雪梅被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">董斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西公民，网名“南柯舟”。自<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日发出消息称被警方控制在医院，被逼删除推文，此后失联至今，情况不明。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月初，董斌在第一时间确认泼墨女孩董瑶琼的身份，并提供其个人、家庭信息，于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被山西国保以“利用手机、电脑使用境外推特软件声援泼墨行动，扰乱公共秩序罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，董斌在得知董瑶琼被送入精神病院后，在推特上发起了拯救董瑶琼的联署行动，于<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被抓捕，山西当局以“在社交软件上发表不实言论，散布谣言，扰乱公共秩序罪”将其再次行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，董斌被正式批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，他被忻府区法院以“寻衅滋事罪”判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月监禁，并被强制删除全部推文。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，董斌出狱。他顶着压力上推特，控诉在狱中曾遭受的酷刑。当局对他的严密监，派出所治安员紧盯，不许离家，他连看病就医的自由也被剥夺。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，董斌在推特发文，控诉当局对他限制出境。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，董斌再在推特发文呼吁勿忘被关精神病院的董瑶琼，在新年到来之际给她写贺年信件。<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，他发出的最后一条消息：“被公安政府五人以上困在医院，逼我删除全部推文”，此后一直失联。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，推特账号<span lang="EN-US"> @realNankezhou </span>显示被冻结。一直处于强迫失踪状态，毫无音信。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董梅：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省沈阳市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，原沈阳翰皇酒店会计，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共邪党开始疯狂迫害法轮功后，董梅曾被非法关押到洗脑班、劳教所遭受酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，董梅和其母亲张筠（<span lang="EN-US">75</span>岁）又被沈阳市沈河区公安分局国保大队抓捕，并被抄家。后董梅被关押在沈阳市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被沈阳市沈河区法院庭审；后获悉董梅被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">董美英：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏省太仓市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，董美英被太仓<span lang="EN-US">610</span>国保警察绑架。同时被绑架的法轮功学员还有秦艳秋与陈永林。秦艳秋、董美英<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<a name="_Hlk52021054"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></a></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52021054;"><a name="_Hlk52327116"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董文秀</span></b></a></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52021054;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52021054;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省哈尔滨香坊区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1961</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被哈尔滨市铁路运输法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。</span></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">董瑶琼：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1989</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日出生，湖南省株洲市攸县桃水镇人，原上海房地产公司中介职员，推特名：<span lang="EN-US">feefeefly</span>，人称“泼墨女孩”，政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾因用<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>在上海市海航大厦前直播其对中共独裁专制的不满，并批评当局对百姓实施洗脑逼迫，随对中共最高领导人习近平的头像泼洒墨汁，进而引起社会广泛热议；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，其被上海市警方抓捕，自此失联，其推特账号被人关闭；<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，被上海市警方送回湖南省攸县老家，并以疑有“精神病”为由被变相关押于株洲市第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>医院，直至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日其父在株洲市第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>医院与女儿见面之后，方知其泼墨行为已被当局定性为“攻击国家领导人”；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，取保释放，并被送到湖南省攸县桃水镇母亲住处；据悉，拘押期间其备受酷刑虐待，父亲董建彪<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日与其相见时，才知其被关押在精神病院时曾被强迫吃药，获释时已完全判若两人，由原先的活泼开朗变成沉默寡言、神情紧张且有些痴呆的样子；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其父亲发出信息，称女儿被再次关进株洲<span lang="EN-US">3</span>医院。后董瑶琼被在株洲<span lang="EN-US">3</span>医院关押两个月后出院。父亲称：董瑶琼出院后比之前情况更加严重，令人十分痛苦。董瑶琼<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日在<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>发布最新视频控诉<span lang="EN-US">"</span>被精神病<span lang="EN-US">"</span>后遭全面监控的情况，随后遭当地国保上门，随后其发的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个推文已经全部消失。本人已被当局控制。音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">前纽约时报摄影记者、纪录片制作人、作家，杜斌于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日早上<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时左右起失联，当晚<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时许，杜斌妹妹接到警方电话告知，已以寻衅滋事罪对杜斌进行拘留，现关押在大兴区拘留所。据了解，本年中警方多次找杜斌问话，称奉国保之命，要求他删除推特上的推文，并打听他是不是还在写书。杜斌让他们自己删，并答应停用推特。近年专注历史方面的研究及资料整理工作，于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>出版《长春饿殍战》，记录<span lang="EN-US">70</span>年前，中共围困长春致数十万人饿死的历史，并仍继续在就相关题目作资料搜集及研究。他又撰写《赤色恐怖：列宁的共产主义实验》，并计划于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月面世。于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，他曾撰写《天安门屠杀》，是第<span lang="EN-US">1</span>本由身处中国内地人士编着的记录<span lang="EN-US">64</span>屠杀的书籍，由杜斌长年在旧书市场搜集大量散落在中国民间的<span lang="EN-US">"64"</span>资料整理而成。本次对杜斌的抓捕，未知是否与他的出版计划有关 。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜二伟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">生于<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年，山西省忻州市代县人，曾于生活晨报、山西青年报、新华社山西分社、发展导报、中国经济时报、中国现代企业报、民主与法制时报等新闻单位任职；前《发展导报》舆论监督部主任、前新华社山西分社《决策参考》工作部主任、前《中国现代企业报》企业观察周刊主编、前《民主与法制时报》经济版主编，新闻媒体人，中国在押政治犯。曾因在网上发表事政言论，在微信上就中共当局“七不准”、“国进民退”、“延迟养老” 及习近平修宪等内容发表批评性言论，而于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被山西省太原市警方强行传唤，并被问及“驱逐低端人口、非洲猪瘟、修宪领导人玩无限期连任”等问题；审讯中曾遭酷刑虐待（如被铐在审讯椅上长达<span lang="EN-US">15</span>小时，戴背铐及脚镣等）；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，又被北京警方抓捕，并交太原市警方被以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，被太原市检察院以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其因言获罪案在山西省太原市迎泽区法院开庭受理，检察院建议法院对其量刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半—<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，至今未予宣判。目前被羁押于太原市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜桂兰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省围场县法轮功学员。二零一八年十一月，河北省公安厅指示承德市公安局，对围场县法轮功学员展开侦查，围场县公安受案，与承德市公安组成“<span lang="EN-US">121</span>”专案组（十二月一日成立），对全县法轮功学员监视七个多月，密谋迫害。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，杜桂兰等三十四名法轮功学员正在集体学法，遭承德市及围场县两地公安局警察抓捕。抓捕后的第二天，开始抄家，抄走大量的书籍、设备等私人物品。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被滦平县法院开庭，杜桂兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜贺先：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河北雄县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下午，杜贺先被雄县公安局国保警察抓捕。后杜贺先被保定市中院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，于<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，被从保定看守所转到石家庄女子监狱关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">杜金花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">上海维权人士。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜金花原住在上海市浦东新区机场镇。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，由于上海浦东国际机场二期项目，杜金花成了受害者、被拆迁人、失地农民。杜金花上访维权<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多年来未得到安置房子和补偿。多次去北京举报控告，至今没有相关部门解决问题。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">10</span>时左右，浦东新区杜金花在家里做中饭，突然被上海市公安局浦东分局川沙派出所警察没有任何法律手续强制带到川沙派出所，被构陷“寻衅滋事罪”刑事拘留，关押在浦东新区看守所。目前案件讯息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜全村：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省庆云县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，山东省庆云县公安局国保大队纠集几十个警察，抓捕了正在学习法轮大法著作的<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多名法轮功学员。根据长期电话监听和监控，警察又抓捕<span lang="EN-US">10</span>余人，共计<span lang="EN-US">46</span>人，其中大多数是<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁以上的老人，大部份法轮功学员被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午，在庆云县法院，夏津县法院人员对六名仍被关押的庆云法轮功学员，赵俊香、王素娟、杜全村、段桂霞、于炳兰、张连云庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，山东夏津县法院开出判决书：赵俊香判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，杜全村判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，王素娟判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，于炳兰判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，张连云判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。杜全村刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜挺：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1966</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，本科学历，原籍甘肃，<span lang="EN-US">1993</span>年左右到上海工作。上海市法轮功学员。因修炼法轮功曾被冤狱<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年迫害。这一次因给人<span lang="EN-US">1</span>本法轮功小册子和<span lang="EN-US">1</span>张写有“法轮大法好 真善忍好”<span lang="EN-US">9</span>字真言的纸条，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，杜挺被普陀分局国保警察和万里派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，杜挺被普陀区检察院批捕，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，被普陀区检察院起诉至普陀区法院。由于所谓法院管辖权的归属，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月中旬，杜挺被构陷案移交至静安区法院受理。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，杜挺被庭审，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">杜晓静：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东庆云县法轮功学员，杜晓静是被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年的杜全村的女儿。杜晓静在无棣县一餐馆打工，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底给到饭馆吃饭顾客讲真相，被顾客恶告，无棣县公安局警察将杜晓静抓捕，直接关押到德州看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月底。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜泽洲：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东济南法轮功学员。战玉彩的丈夫，大学文化。因坚持修炼法轮功，遭到中共的多次迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月份被公安劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，关押在位于济南刘长山路的原济南市劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日遭到济南泉城路派出所警察抓捕，被关押到济南看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年被劳教关押在章丘的山东省第二男子劳教所迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被济南长清区公安警察跟踪抓捕。在长清区 “<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”、长清区公安国保大队的操控、指示下，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月法轮功学员杜泽洲被长清区法院判<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年有期徒刑，现关押在山东省监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">杜以合：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山东省临沂市沂南县法轮功学员，杜以合<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十六岁，家住沂南县苏村镇东菜园村，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被非法劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年“青岛峰会”前，他从外地打工回家，沂南公安局和苏村派出所警察多次上门骚扰他的正常生活，不允许他出去打工。<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日“为防止他外出打工”，警察入室抓捕了他。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被沂南法院在沂南看守所秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，在山东省济南监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">段守珍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：武汉市青山区人，法轮功学员。因信法轮功被长期监控和受到打压迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，当其在武汉市汉口区金家墩邮局附近宣传法轮功时，遭到青山区公安分局郑珂的构陷，随被武汉市汉口区警方刑拘，<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月其案件被转至武汉市青山区检察院。期间因证据不足，青山区检察院两次退侦，要求补充资料。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日其案件已转至武汉市青山区法院，武汉市青山区法院于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日庭审，至今刑期未知。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">段天俊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽合肥市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日，段天俊陪妻子去拿药（他妻子是几年前段天俊被迫害时惊吓过度造成精神出现问题），被合肥市滨湖派出所便衣跟踪抓捕，后强行闯入家中非法抄家。段天俊之妻潘能存虽未修炼法轮功，也被指控：因为陪伴丈夫段天俊外出时，段天俊发了救人真相传单，而被拘役六个月，缓刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月。而段天俊被合肥市蜀山区法院非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，之前因其已被羁押过一年九个月，故刑期为：</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">26</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日～</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">月</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">28</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">日。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">段学琴：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">内蒙古赤峰市巴林左旗法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，段学琴在巴林右旗发放法轮功台历时，被巴林右旗公安警察抓捕。后被抄家。段学琴多次遭惨无人道迫害，这次出狱不到一年，又被抓捕，日前被巴林右旗法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。段学琴被关押在巴林右旗看守所期间，曾被电击，被迫害的身体非常虚弱，在十多天以前被非法庭审时她是坐着轮椅被推进法庭的。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">多吉扎西（藏）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">西藏拉萨著名商人、民营企业家、神湖集团创办人多吉扎西于<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年被不公开审判，判处无期徒刑。</b>现西藏自治区法院给多吉扎西定的罪名是“贷款诈骗罪”，然而，该案疑点是，涉案金额仅仅<span lang="EN-US">150</span>万元。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，北京法律界专家论证结果是，多吉扎西无法认定犯有贷款诈骗罪，仅仅犯挪用资金罪。并建议西藏自治区法院改判有期徒刑。据了解，多吉扎西在狱中坚持不认罪，一直苦苦等待冤案平反，而多吉扎西的哥哥因多次为弟上访，已被西藏维稳部门禁止离开拉萨市。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年多吉扎西的亲人已聘请北京泽博律师事务所的王飞律师为其辩护。王飞前往拉萨后，在多次请求下，终于获得监狱方面探视机会。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">多杰扎才（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生不详，西藏那曲地区比如县达塘乡央唐区<span lang="EN-US">4</span>村人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日在拉萨市被拉萨警方拘捕，后被以涉嫌多项罪名正式逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日获知，其被以拉萨市中级法院以“阻止政府在‘纳拉赞巴’圣上开矿”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，以“私下向他人贷款罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，以“妨碍公务罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，数罪并罚，最终执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">11</span>年。目前被关押在拉萨扎其监狱。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">E.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 22.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">F.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">樊钧益、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范路杰、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">范明兰、范士荣、范文成、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">范一平</span>、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">方斌、方芳、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">方宗菊</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯宝定、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯俊苓</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、冯群豪、冯少勇、冯小妹、冯蕴青、丰晓燕、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">付常国、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付秋荣</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">付文花、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">傅炫娟、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">樊钧益：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南长沙民主人士，网名铁子。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年“六四”前夕被刑拘，被捕原因与其长期从事墙外信息搬运工作有关，其本人创建的微信公民群及<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群，群友一度达到两三千人，目前猜测当局可能担忧其“六四”有所动作而将其刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">48</span>岁的樊钧益早年曾组织、参与多种公益活动，包括关爱山区学童、定时组织探望敬老院老人及参与公益百公里志愿者活动等，系一名忠实的“中国国民党”粉丝，并自称该党“精神党员”。长期坚持利用翻墙软件了解国际媒体报道，并将消息转发至墙内，在由其创建的微信群和<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群传发，亦曾多处组织参与举牌活动，并因此被警方多次拘留处罚。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范路杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江西九江市法轮功学员。家住江西九江市浔阳区。<span lang="EN-US">1955</span>年生。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月之后，范路杰被浔阳区公安分局劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次，第一次是<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半；第二次是<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月；第三次是<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年五月被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，总计被劳教<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。三次劳教都是被关押在九江市马家垄劳教所。期间，范路杰一直被包夹，强迫劳动，吃饭、睡觉、上厕所都被人跟着，不许跟其他法轮功学员接触，不准自由说话。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被濂溪区公安分局警察抓捕，一直被关押在九江看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月传出，仅靠一段模糊不清的监控视频，范路杰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">范明兰<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省延吉市法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月开始修炼法轮功，因坚持信仰<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年被劳教<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。后被数次抓捕，曾遭酷刑折磨。范明兰<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日左右又被延边州龙井市警察抓捕，七月末家人获悉，她被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">范士荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生。法轮功学员，医生。本在广东省潮州市饶平县康民医院工作，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被警方绑架，目前被非法关押浙江丽水看守所。看守所不允许她看医生，疫情期间不允许亲友存衣物，不允许律师会见，家属给存的钱也不让花。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，范士荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范文成：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州<span lang="EN-US">11.12</span>大抓捕被抓人员。广州国安局以颠覆国家政权为由，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在广州对民运人士进行了大抓捕，目前已有四人被抓捕，分别是：范一平、范文成、赖见君、乔莲红。被抓后，即遭指定监视居住，罪名是颠覆国家政权。<b><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">范一平：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">广州<span lang="EN-US">11.12</span>大抓捕被抓人员。广州国安局以颠覆国家政权为由，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日在广州对民运人士进行了大抓捕，目前已有四人被抓捕，分别是：范一平、范文成、赖见君、乔莲红。范一平是广州自民主墙时期的老民运，<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年初曾接待秘密回国发动组党的王炳章，后以帮助王希哲流亡而被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。此次被抓后，即遭指定监视居住，罪名是颠覆国家政权。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">方斌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉人，公民记者，武汉公民记者方斌被人们誉为“活着的吹哨人”，方斌因为直播武汉疫情于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日晚上被武汉警方强行入户，在没有搜查证的情况下，对其家中电脑、手机扣押。方斌<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日以手机直播的方式去了武汉几家医院，因其在五医院的几分钟时间无意发现殡仪馆运送八具尸体堆放，此视频引起海内外舆论震动。后，方斌在视频上向全世界公开宣示<span lang="EN-US">:</span>号召国人起来全民自救、推翻暴政，开展全民反抗运动。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日下午遭到武汉警方破门抓捕。至今音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">方芳：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁大连法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日被取保候审。后<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月八名法轮功学员被大连开发区法院判刑：周海燕<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，胡志琴<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年半，来桂芳<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，时宁瑶<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，林景萍<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，方芳<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，郝福奎<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，贾秀春<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。方芳刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">方宗菊：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，方宗菊在安陆市区讲法轮功被抓捕，被抄家。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日被安陆市法院庭审，多日后得知她被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，冯宝定因在“昆钢”（昆明钢铁控股有限公司）粘贴“法轮大法好”标语，被中共抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日被昆明市西山区法院开庭。<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，冯宝定在安宁市看守所收到判决，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并勒索罚金一千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">冯俊苓：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">天津市滨海新区大港街法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，天津市公安局出动大批警察与各区级公安分局和下属派出所在全市抓捕法轮功学员。包括冯俊苓在内的</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">37</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。所有被迫害的法轮功学员几乎均被抄家。至少</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">14</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">人被非法批捕，目前已知有</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">10</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">人已被冤判入狱，最高刑期达</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">11</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年。冯俊苓<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年被庭审，检方曾建议量刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月获悉，冯俊苓被冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯群豪：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳销售圣经播放器案被捕人员之一。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日出生，汉族，初中毕业，住所地为广东省肇庆市四会市东城街道陶冲村；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市生命树文化传播有限公司是一家成立于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月的合法企业。因销售圣经播放器，竟然导致傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒被逮捕。中共当局于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，以所谓非法经营罪将他们抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位基督徒都被关押在深圳九围看守所。其家人和律师都被威胁，不得透露案情。后获悉，冯群豪被法院判处</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">3</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年有期徒刑，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯少勇：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">1971</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月出生，湖北省仙桃市张沟镇人，北京邮电大学博士，前北京邮电大学，广东省深圳市龙岗区长住居民，原深圳市某中学员工，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早年曾在北京邮电大学读博士生，为人乐观谦和，人缘好，因是研究项目组技术骨干，曾于<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年在该校与同事成功研发机顶盒，并将个人所获奖金<span lang="EN-US">100</span>万全部捐给该校；但因信仰、宣传法轮功，遭中共北京当局严厉打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，其被深圳市龙岗区警方突然抓捕，次日被刑事拘留，并被送深圳市龙岗区看守所关押，其所在中学办公室、宿舍，其家及亲戚家当天均被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，被以涉嫌“邪教罪”转正式逮捕，控其与另一法轮功友人陈泽奇“均系法轮功组织成员，二人利用掌握的专业知识，组装伪基站给他人，并使用伪基站宣传法轮功”，属于违法行为；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其案件被深圳市龙岗区法院开庭受理，至<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，其被深圳市龙岗法院一审以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；其不服上诉，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日经深圳市中级人民法院终审裁定，驳回上诉、维持原判，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。目前在广东省四会监狱服刑。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯小妹：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">江苏无锡市滨湖区拆迁受害者冯小妹，因被起诉于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日再次被无锡市滨湖区人民法院以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”批准逮捕，现羁押在无锡市第二看守所。冯小妹因房屋拆迁和家中财物被抢等问题，在当地始终无法解决，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日到北京天安门裸奔维权，被当地公安人员带回后以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘。在被非法羁押<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月后，于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日被无锡市公安局滨湖分局批准逮捕，在关押期间，冯小妹被两次强迫做精神病鉴定，其家人多次前往交涉无果，之后因为滨湖区雪浪街道要跟冯小妹谈拆迁问题，于是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日将她取保候审释放回家。在取保期间，冯小妹并未进京上访维权，却于<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日又被滨湖区法院以同样罪名批准逮捕关押。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日开庭。后判决讯息全无。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">冯蕴青：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">武汉法轮功学员。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被绑架，关押在武汉东西湖区武汉第一看守所。参与绑架和扣押的部门有：武汉市网监支队，武汉市“国保”支队，江岸区公安分局后湖派出所。冯蕴青于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被武汉市汉阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，冯蕴青不服判决，上诉到武汉市法院，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月武汉中级法院二审维持原判。现在冯蕴青被非法关押在武汉女子监狱（位于武汉市宝丰路）。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">丰晓燕：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">毕业于山东师范大学新闻系，临沂市人大副调研员，副县级。二十多年公职期间因不满现有体制不被提拔，不允出国，不准考取研究生博士职称学历，<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年被市政府组织黑社会撞断腰，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年春天退党退公职，单位拒绝。同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月公开支持香港反送中，被送进派出所拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年新冠疫情间对体制内失察渎职，捐款贪污，罔顾人命，胡作非为忍无可忍，故上京发声。却被侮辱为精神病并强制治疗。丰晓燕拒不认罪，于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被送至临沂第四精神病院，北京路育才路派出所二十多位警察，将患有腰椎间盘突出的丰晓燕在水泥地板拖行至住院部三楼，未进行精神检测，强行关进精神病医院。污蔑其为精神分裂症并强制用药。一直关押在精神病医院。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">付常国：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> 1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，广东省深圳市人，“打工者中心劳动力”（<span lang="EN-US">Worker Empowerment</span>）工作人员，劳动法律咨询者，公益维权者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">自<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年始，其所在打工者中心以开展公益事业为己任，每年为至少<span lang="EN-US">500</span>名企业外来打工者提供免费法律咨询，举办超过<span lang="EN-US">200</span>余次免费文娱学习活动，使至少十万名工友受惠，因其亦参与其中，遂倍受基层工友的广泛欢迎；自<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年以来，因焊接设备制造商深圳佳士科技<span lang="EN-US">(Jasic Technology)</span>与员工发生劳资冲突，佳士员工愤起维权抗议，其代表“打工者中心”前往调查介入，并与另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名佳士工友积极尝试在中国大陆组建工会（类似于欧美国家里专门为工人谋福利的“工会”，而非“中华全国总工会”），遂遭到当局的严厉打击，被深圳警方多次传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，参与组建工会的<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名工人因“试图成立非法工会”而被警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”拘押，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其因在警察局门外喊口号声援被抓工人，故而亦被深圳市坪山区警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，又被以涉嫌“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”正式逮捕；据悉，其姐付红娥曾于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日为其递交“取保候审申请书”遭拒，理由是一旦批准申请，就“可能毁灭、伪造证据，干扰证人作证或者串供”，<span lang="EN-US">2019 </span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US"> 1</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日又在深圳市第二看守所给其汇款后被“查无此人”退回，迄今不予释放。目前被羁押于深圳市第二看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">付秋荣：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省烟台市龙口法轮功学员。袁玉芹、姚新人、<a name="_Hlk52325542">付秋荣</a><span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被国保跟踪抓捕。身强力壮的姚新人<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，在龙口市张家沟看守所「突发」脑溢血，在龙口市人民医院被做开颅手术和气管切开术，龙口公安安插四五个警察在医院进行二十四小时监视。姚新人成植物人状态。龙口公安、国保、看守所至今没给家属任何解释。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，袁玉芹被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，付秋荣被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。付秋荣刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">付文花：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">湖北省南漳县武安镇人，因为<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月她儿子付学刚遭遇车祸后对方不承担医疗费，交警不予处理让他到法院起诉而上访，上访期间被对此殴打、拘留<span lang="EN-US">,</span>曾在拘留所被迫割腕自尽。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日付文花在京被南漳县武安镇派出所强行押回后被拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，关押在南漳拘留所。<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午武安镇政府李才明书记和几个不明身份人员强行将付文花从南漳拘留所抬出来塞进车里带走，进行私自拘禁、酷刑虐待并讹诈，<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日付文花被折磨至昏死而丢在路旁被人救起。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，付文花被南漳县公安局抓走，关押在湖北省南漳县看守所。付文花于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">3</span>点在南漳县法院秘密开庭，被以寻衅滋事罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">傅炫娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳销售圣经播放器案被捕人员之一。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1978</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，汉族，中专学历，原籍地是广西壮族自治区北海市合浦县常乐镇大教村；</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">深圳市生命树文化传播有限公司是一家成立于<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月的合法企业。因销售圣经播放器，竟然导致傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等四基督徒被逮捕。中共当局于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，以所谓非法经营罪将他们抓走，<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月遭正式逮捕。目前傅炫娟、邓天永、韩丽、冯群豪等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>位基督徒都被关押在深圳九围看守所。其家人和律师都被威胁，不得透露案情。后获悉法院</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">判处傅炫娟有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p> <p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p>
</div>
